       <section class="ow-content"> 
        <div class="ow-body-text"> 
         <h2 class="ow-heading ow-heading-1 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-1 ow-headinghelper-1">Make meetings inclusive and interactive for everyone</h2> 
         <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-1 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
          <p>Help remote participants feel as engaged and empowered to participate in meetings as those in the room.</p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2 ow-toggle-ctn"> 
          <div class="ow-4-toggles ow-toggles" data-active="0" role="tablist"> 
           <div aria-hidden="true" class="ow-theme-bg ow-toggle-bg"></div> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-0 office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-media-0" aria-selected="true" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-0" id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-0" role="tab" tabindex="0"> <span>Live captions</span> </button> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-1 office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-media-1" aria-selected="false" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-1" id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-1" role="tab" tabindex="-1"> <span>Raise hand</span> </button> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-2 office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-media-2" aria-selected="false" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-2" id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-2" role="tab" tabindex="-1"> <span>Whiteboard</span> </button> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-3 office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-media-3" aria-selected="false" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-3" id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-3" role="tab" tabindex="-1"> <span>Intelligent capture</span> </button> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-0" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-0" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
           <p>See a real-time text stream as participants speak during a meeting.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-1" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" hidden id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-1" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
           <p>Let everyone know you want to speak, simply by pressing a button.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-toggle-2" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" hidden id="office-TriToggle-vfuynsz-text-2" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">

       <section class="m-area-heading ow-sticky-nav-dock"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading-3 ow-headinghelper-1 ">Easy to use and hassle free</h2> 
        <div data-grid="col-12"> 
         <div class="c-paragraph"> 
          <p>Create friction-free meeting spaces. Easily start or join a meeting, share ideas and content, and allow people to meet without distractions.</p> 
         </div>

       <section class="ow-content"> 
        <div class="ow-body-text"> 
         <h2 class="ow-heading ow-heading-1 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-1 ow-headinghelper-1">Bring Microsoft Teams to any meeting space</h2> 
         <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-1 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
          <p>Meet the needs of any size space with a wide selection of Teams Rooms devices.</p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2 ow-toggle-ctn"> 
          <div class="ow-4-toggles ow-toggles" data-active="0" role="tablist"> 
           <div aria-hidden="true" class="ow-theme-bg ow-toggle-bg"></div> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-0 office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-media-0" aria-selected="true" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-0" id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-0" role="tab" tabindex="0"> <span>Teams Rooms</span> </button> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-1 office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-media-1" aria-selected="false" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-1" id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-1" role="tab" tabindex="-1"> <span>Focus Room</span> </button> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-2 office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-media-2" aria-selected="false" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-2" id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-2" role="tab" tabindex="-1"> <span>Medium Space</span> </button> <button aria-controls="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-3 office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-media-3" aria-selected="false" class="ow-hidden-focus ow-toggle ow-toggle-3" id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-3" role="tab" tabindex="-1"> <span>Large Space</span> </button> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-0" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-0" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
           <p>Microsoft Teams Rooms bridge the gap between in-person and remote attendees, so everyone can be seen, heard, and fully participate  whether they are working in small, medium or large meeting spaces.</p> 
          </div> 
          <div class="ow-link-wrapper"> <a href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=2162666&amp;clcid=0x409&amp;culture=en-us&amp;country=US" class="c-call-to-action c-glyph f-lightweight ow-link ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2" aria-label="Explore more information about devices for Teams Rooms." target="_blank" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;WhatdevicesareintheseTeamsRooms&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;n1m1r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r6a2&quot;,&quot;tags&quot;:{&quot;BiLinkName&quot;:&quot;WhatdevicesareintheseTeamsRooms&quot;}}"> <span> What Teams Rooms devices are in this video? </span> </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-1" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" hidden id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-1" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
           <p>Ideate and collaborate in spaces ideal for three to five people.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-2" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" hidden id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-2" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
           <p>Share ideas and connect with up to eleven people in the room, and many more online.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-3" class="ow-body-panel ow-panel" hidden id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-text-3" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
          <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
           <p>Designed to seat eighteen or more people, large meeting spaces are great for formal presentations, large team gatherings, and collaboration across work groups.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div aria-describedby="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-toggle-0" class="ow-media ow-panel" id="office-TriToggle-bn8uc2c-media-0" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0"> 
         <div class="ow-media-ctn ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-3"> 
          <div class="ow-video-player-container fluid-iframe"> <iframe frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="true" src="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/videoplayer/embed/RWDIk3?autoplay=false&amp;loop=false&amp;mute=false&amp;controls=true&amp;playPauseTrigger=false" title="R&amp;F_Microsoft_TeamsRooms_Video02"></iframe> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="ow-paragraph ow-paragraph-2 ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2">
          <p>Microsoft Teams Rooms bridge the gap between in-person and remote attendees, so everyone can be seen, heard, and fully participate  whether they are working in small, medium or large meeting spaces.</p> 
         </div>

        </div>

   <div id="primaryR20" data-grid="container" data-region-key="primaryr20" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;primaryR20 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
    <div id="office-ContentAreaHeadingTemplate-njol7nz" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;R20officecontentareaheadings 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_office-ContentAreaHeadingTemplate&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r12a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.AllModulesTools|primaryR20|coreui-region|office-ContentAreaHeadingTemplate-njol7nz|office-ContentAreaHeadingTemplate"> 
     <div class="ow-content-area-heading x-clearfix ow-wrap-ctas" data-is-full-bleed="True"> 
      <div class=" white Left Slim Full-bleed" data-grid="col-12"> 
       <section class="m-area-heading ow-sticky-nav-dock"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading-3 ow-headinghelper-1 ">Frequently asked questions</h2> 
        <div data-grid="col-12"> 
        </div> 
       </section> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;R20CollapseDrawer 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r12a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.AllModulesTools|primaryR20|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
     <section class="cui-drawer"> 
      <div class="cui-header "> 
       <div class="cui-drawer-toggle"> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Expand all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="f-expand c-action-toggle" name="Expand all" data-toggled-label="Expand all" aria-label="Expand all">Expand all</button> <span>|</span> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Collapse all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="f-collapse c-action-toggle" name="Collapse all" data-toggled-label="Collapse all" aria-label="Collapse all" disabled>Collapse all</button> 
       </div> 
       <div style="clear: both;"></div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer0">What are Microsoft Teams Rooms?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft Teams Rooms are purpose-built calling and meeting room solutions that deliver a native Microsoft Teams experience with HD audio and video, on Teams-certified hardware from Microsoft and Microsoft partners (Microsoft Surface Hub, Crestron, Dell, HP, Lenovo, Logitech, Poly, and Yealink). Teams Rooms deliver consistent, intuitive, and inclusive meeting experiences.</p> 
        <p>The Teams Rooms experience is available on select modular, integrated, or all-in-one Teams-certified devices. &nbsp;Modular solutions consist of a touch-panel control in the center of the room that allows you to manage the meeting without leaving your seat. These solutions can pair with certified A/V peripherals enabling customizable configurations that scale to any room size. Integrated solutions are designed for smaller spaces and bring together the speakers, microphones, camera, and computer into a single device that can be mounted on any display. Microsoft certifies hardware and peripherals from industry-leading device manufacturers for use with Microsoft Teams, to ensure reliable, high-quality audio and video experiences.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer1">How do the Microsoft Teams Rooms Standard and Premium licenses align to Microsoft Teams Rooms?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft Teams Rooms Standard and Premium enable all the licenses needed for Microsoft Teams Rooms while providing customers with two options to manage their devices.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer2">What devices are certified for Microsoft Teams?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>See a list of certified <a aria-label="Explore a list of certified Microsoft Teams Rooms devices." href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-teams/across-devices/devices/category?devicetype=20" class="c-hyperlink">Microsoft Teams Rooms devices</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer3">How much does Microsoft Teams Rooms Premium cost?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft Teams Rooms Premium is $50 per device per month.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer4">How much does Microsoft Teams Rooms Standard cost?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft Teams Rooms Standard is $15 per device per month.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer5">What are the benefits of the managed service included in Microsoft Teams Rooms Premium?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>The managed service enhances the meeting room management experience through expert operations, requiring less time and resources from your IT team. The service provides recommendations from our team, proactive management on your behalf, and knowledge from our entire customer network to ensure you get the most from your environment. This proactive approach to room operations maintains optimal meeting experiences across sites and promotes user satisfaction.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m2r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer6">Can I try Microsoft Teams Rooms Standard and Premium before purchasing?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-wwkqnt8-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Yes, customers can sign up for a free trial of both licenses in the Microsoft 365 admin portal.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </section> 
    </div>

        <div data-grid="stack-3" class="ow-width-100per mobile-overlay  xs-ow-bgc-ffffff  l-ow-bgc-trans ow-hero-content  l-ow-cl-fff"> 
         <div data-grid="col-8" class="ow-hero-text-wrapper ow-has-paragraph"> 
          <h2 class="c-heading-2 x-weight-semibold ow-pb-00 ow-mb-5 ow-headinghelper-1">Microsoft Teams Rooms</h2> 
          <div class="c-paragraph ow-mt-00"> 
           <div data-ow-marketselector="true">
            <p>Help ensure everyone can fully participate from anywhere.</p> 
           </div>
